function checkbox_limit(name){
    $(':checkbox[name="'+name+'"]').click(function(){$(this).blur();});
    $(':checkbox[name="'+name+'"]').formValidator({tipid: name + "_Tip",onfocus:""}).functionValidator({fun:function(){
        var len = $(':checkbox[name="'+name+'"]:checked').length;
        if(len &gt; 4) return '最多选择四项';
        return true;
    }, onerror:''});
}

         fun: function(val, elem) {
             var price=$.trim($("#MinPrice3").val());
             var price_rex=/^[0-9]{1,5}$/;
             if(price.length==0 || price == 0){
                 return "请填写门市价";

                 return "价格必须为数字，最多填写填写5位";

           var price2=$.trim($("#MinPrice1").val());

             return "价格必须为数字";

           return true;

//设置默认值
function setDefaultValue(id,value){
  if(value!=''){
    $("#"+id).val(value);
  }
}
//解析并设置行程安排隐藏表单域
function setXingChengAnPai(value,showId,type){
  if(value=='') return;
  var valueStr = value.split("^");
  for(var i=0;i&lt;valueStr.length;i++){
    if(valueStr[i]!=''){
      if(0==type)
    	  $("#"+showId+"_"+i).val(valueStr[i].substring((i+"_").length));
      if(1==type)
        $("#"+valueStr[i]).attr("checked",true);
    } 
  }
}
//获取行程安排值并设置隐藏表单域
function getXingChengAnPai(textId,valueId,type){
   var hidden_value='';
   $(textId).each(function(i){
     if(1==type){
      var id=$(this).attr("id");
      hidden_value+=id+"^"
     }else{
      if($(this).val()!='')
        hidden_value+=i+'_'+$(this).val()+"^";
     }
   });
   $("#"+valueId).val(hidden_value);
}
// 创建分隔元素：元素name、默认值、最大长度、分隔符、单条最多个数
function createSplitElem(elemName, defaultVal, maxlen, splitchar, singleLen, isreadonly) {
    var arr = [];
    arr.push('&lt;input type="hidden" id="' + elemName + '" name="' + elemName + '"  /&gt;');
    var arrVal = defaultVal.split(splitchar);
    $(arrVal).each(function(i, n) {
      var removeHtml='&lt;a id="remove_' + elemName + '_' + i + '" href="javascript:void(removeTextBox(\''+elemName+'\','+maxlen+',\''  +elemName + '_' + i + '\'));"&gt;&nbsp;移除&nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;';
        if (isreadonly == true) {
            arr.push('&lt;input type="text" id="' + elemName + '_' + i + '" para-name="' + elemName + '" value="' + n + '" class="text5" readonly="true" maxlength="' + singleLen + '"&gt;'+(i!=0?removeHtml:''));
        }
        else {
            arr.push('&lt;input type="text" id="' + elemName + '_' + i + '" para-name="' + elemName + '" value="' + n + '" class="text5" maxlength="' + singleLen + '" onblur="checkRepeater(this,'+i+')"&gt;');
        }
        if (i == maxlen - 1) {
            return false;
        }
    });
    var str = arr.join("");
    $('span[para-name=' + elemName + ']').append(str).append('&lt;a id="_addTextBox" href="javascript:void(addTextBox(\'' + elemName + '\', ' + maxlen + ', \'' + splitchar + '\', ' + singleLen + ', ' + isreadonly + '));"&gt;增加&lt;/a&gt;');
    if(arrVal.length==maxlen){
    	$('#_addTextBox').attr("style","display:none");
    }
    joinEvent(elemName, splitchar);
}
// 新增日期文本框
function addTextBox(elemName, maxlen, splitchar, singleLen, isreadonly) {
    var arr = [];
    var objs = $(':input[para-name="' + elemName + '"]');
    var len = objs.length;
    if (len &gt;= maxlen) return;
    if(len==maxlen-1){
         $('#_addTextBox').attr("style","display:none");
    }
    var removeHtml='&lt;a id="remove_' + elemName + '_' + len + '" href="javascript:void(removeTextBox(\''+elemName+'\','+maxlen+',\''  +elemName + '_' + len + '\'));"&gt;&nbsp;移除&nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;';
    if (isreadonly == true) {
        arr.push('&lt;input type="text" id="' + elemName + '_' + len + '" para-name="' + elemName + '" value="" class="text5" readonly="true" maxlength="' + singleLen + '"&gt;'+removeHtml);
    } else {
      arr.push('&lt;input type="text" id="' + elemName + '_' + len + '" para-name="' + elemName + '" value="" class="text5" maxlength="' + singleLen + '" onblur="checkRepeater(this,'+len+')"&gt;'+removeHtml);
    }
    var str = arr.join('');
    $('#_addTextBox').before(str);
    joinEvent(elemName, splitchar);
}
//移除日期文本框
function removeTextBox(elemName,maxlen,id){
	var objs = $(':input[para-name="'+elemName+'"]');
	var len = objs.length;
	if(len==maxlen){
	      $('#_addTextBox').attr("style","");
	  }
  $("#"+id).remove();
  $("#remove_"+id).remove();
}
//根据选择的天数动态生成行程表单
function xingchengChange(){
  var day=$("#xingchengtianshuq option:selected").text().replace("日","");
  //行程天数联动
  $("#xingchengtianshuh").val(day-1);
  //如果是默认的2天
  if(day==2){
    $("#_xingchengtianshu").html("");
    return;
  }
  var day_zh_array=new Array('一','二','三','四','五','六','七','八','九','十');
  var xingcheng_html="";
  for(var i=3;i&lt;=day;i++){
    var index=i-1;
    var day_zh='';
    if(i&gt;10){
      day_zh=day_zh_array[day_zh_array.length-1]+day_zh_array[i-10-1];
    }else{
      day_zh=day_zh_array[index];
    }
      xingcheng_html+='&lt;tr&gt;'
      +'&lt;td&gt;第'+day_zh+'天&lt;/td&gt;'
      +'&lt;td&gt;&lt;input id="dangrixingcheng_'+index+'" type="text" value="" maxlength="50" class="txt w277 c_999 mb5" onblur="checkJingdian(this)"&gt;&lt;br&gt;'
      +'&lt;textarea name="xc_'+index+'" class="txtarea w277 c_999 h60" id="xingcheng_'+index+'" onblur="checkXingcheng(this);"&gt;&lt;/textarea&gt;&lt;/td&gt;'
      +'&lt;td&gt;'
      +'&lt;ul class="checklist"&gt;'
                    +'&lt;li&gt;&lt;input type="checkbox" id="yongcan_'+index+'_1" value="1"&gt; &lt;label for="yongcan1"&gt;早餐&lt;/label&gt;&lt;/li&gt;'           +'&lt;li&gt;&lt;input type="checkbox" id="yongcan_'+index+'_2" value="2"&gt; &lt;label for="yongcan2"&gt;午餐&lt;/label&gt;&lt;/li&gt;'           +'&lt;li&gt;&lt;input type="checkbox" id="yongcan_'+index+'_3" value="3"&gt; &lt;label for="yongcan3"&gt;晚餐&lt;/label&gt;&lt;/li&gt;'           +'&lt;/ul&gt;'
          +'&lt;/td&gt;'
          +'&lt;td&gt;&lt;input id="zhusu_'+index+'" type="text" class="txt w120" maxlength="8"&gt;&lt;/td&gt;'
          +'&lt;/tr&gt;';
  }
  $("#_xingchengtianshu").html(xingcheng_html);
  //清除数据
  $("#dangrixingcheng_0").val("请您填写当天途径城市或景点如：北京-上海");
  $("#dangrixingcheng_1").val("请您填写当天途径城市或景点如：北京-上海");
  $("#xingcheng_0").val("请您填写当天行程安排，行程安排应在10-1500字之间，不能填写电话及特殊字符");
  $("#xingcheng_1").val("请您填写当天行程安排，行程安排应在10-1500字之间，不能填写电话及特殊字符");
  
  //加载输入框时间
  for(var i=3;i&lt;=day;i++){
	  var index=i-1;
	  $("#xingcheng_"+index).bind('focus',function(){
              $(this).addClass("h110");
              if($(this).hasClass("h60")){
            	  $(this).removeClass("h60");
              }
            
	   });
	  $("#xingcheng_"+index).bind('blur',function(){
	    	  $(this).addClass("h60");
	    	  if($(this).hasClass("h110")){
            	  $(this).removeClass("h110");
              }
           
	 });
  }
}
// 拼接事件
function joinEvent(elemName, splitChar) {
    var objs = $(':input[para-name="' + elemName + '"]');
    objs.unbind('blur').bind('blur', function() {
        joinValue(elemName, splitChar);
    });
}
// 光标离开时重新拼接值
function joinValue(elemName, splitChar) {
    var arr = [];
    var objs = $(':input[para-name="' + elemName + '"]');
    $(objs).each(function(i, n) {
        if (!!$(n).val()) { 
            arr.push($(n).val());
        }
    });
    var str = arr.join(splitChar);
    $('#' + elemName).val(str);
}
function saveJoinValue(){
  joinValue('riqishuzhi', '、');
}

function guoji_validator(){
	//发团日期
   var index = $(":radio[name='fatuanriqi']:checked").val();
   if (index == 2) {
      $('#riqishuzhi').val('');
      $('#riqishuzhi2').val('');
    }else{
      var v1 = $('#riqishuzhi').val();
      var r = !!v1;
      if (!r) {
          alert("出发日期不能为空");
          $("#riqishuzhi_0").focus();
          return false;
      }  
    }
   
    //行程安排
    var index = $.c.common.getRadioIndex('moshiqiehuan');
    if (index == 1) {
    	$("#jiandanxingchen").val(editNew.getContent());
        var xingchengValue=$.trim($("#jiandanxingchen").val());
        if($.trim(editNew.getContentTxt()).length==0){
        	 alert("请您填写行程安排");
             $("#editor").focus();
        	 return false;
        }
        if($.trim(editNew.getContentTxt()).length&lt;6||$.trim(editNew.getContentTxt()).length&gt;10000){
       	    alert("请您填写行程安排，行程安排应在10-10000字之间，不能填写电话及特殊字符");
            $("#editor").focus();
       	    return false;
         }
    }else{
    	var xingchengLen =$(":textarea[name^='xc_']").length; 
        var xingcheng_regx=/^([\s\S]){10,2000}$/;
        var jingdian_regx=/^([\s\S]){2,15}$/;
        var zhusu_regx=/^([\s\S]){2,8}$/;
        for(var i=0;i&lt;xingchenglen&gt;&lt;6 ||jandanxcy.length&gt;10000){
  	    	$.formValidator.setTipState(null, "onError", '请您填写行程安排，行程安排应在10-10000字之间，不能填写电话及特殊字符', 'jiandanxingchen_Tip');
  	    }else{
  	    	$.formValidator.setTipState(null, "onCorrect", ' ', 'jiandanxingchen_Tip');
  	    	$("#jiandanxingchen").val(editNew.getContent());
  	    }
  	});
 	 
 	 $('#xingchengbiaozhun').hide();
     $('#editor').show();
}

function changeMoshi(initF) {
    var index = $.c.common.getRadioIndex('moshiqiehuan');
   
    if (index == 1) {
    	
    	editNew=getUEEDitor({
    		id:"editor",
    		"defaultTxt":"请您填写行程安排，行程安排应为10-10000字之间，不能填写电话及特殊字符",
    		"autoHeight":true,
    		"width":580,
    		"height":235,
    		"focusHeight":400,
    		"maxWordsLen":10000
    		
    	});
    	
    	
    	 //简单行程安排
    	if(initF==1){
    		editNew.ready(function(){
    		    //需要ready后执行，否则可能报错
    			 editNew.setContent(UE.utils.html($("#jiandanxingchen").val()));
    		   
    		})
    	}
    	 editNew.onblur(function(){
     	    //blur后的处理
     	    var jiandanxc=editNew.getContent();
     	    var jandanxcy=editNew.getContentTxt()
     	    $("#jiandanxingchen").val(jiandanxc);
     	    if(jandanxcy=="" || jandanxcy==" " ||$.trim(jandanxcy)==""){
     	    	$.formValidator.setTipState(null, "onError", '请您填写行程安排', 'jiandanxingchen_Tip');
     	    }else if(jandanxcy.length&lt;6 ||jandanxcy.length&gt;10000){
     	    	$.formValidator.setTipState(null, "onError", '请您填写行程安排，行程安排应在10-10000字之间，不能填写电话及特殊字符', 'jiandanxingchen_Tip');
     	    }else{
     	    	$.formValidator.setTipState(null, "onCorrect", ' ', 'jiandanxingchen_Tip');
     	    	$("#jiandanxingchen").val(editNew.getContent());
     	    }
     	});
    	 
    	 if(!(editNew.body) &amp;&amp; myInfo.infoID == 0){
    		 setTimeout(function(){ delay(initF); }, 0); // 如果第一次编辑框没有出现，再次初始化
         }  
        
    	  $('#xingchengbiaozhun').hide();
          $('#editor').show();
       
    } else {
    	$('#xingchengbiaozhun').show();
        $('#editor').hide();
        $('#jiandanxingchen_Tip').empty();
    }
}

function addDatePick(paraname) {
    var now = new Date();
    var lastdate = new Date(new Date().setDate(now.getDate() + 90));
    $(':text[para-name='+paraname+']').datepick({
        monthsToShow: 2, monthsToStep: 1, showOnFocus: true, yearRange: "-0:+1", minDate: now, maxDate: lastdate, onSelect: function() { $(this).blur(); }
    });
}
//校验途经城市
function checkJingdian(target){
    var regex=/^([\s\S]){2,15}$/;
    check(target, regex);
}
//校验行程
function checkXingcheng(target){
    var regex=/^([\s\S]){10,1500}$/;
    check(target, regex);
    mergeEnterKey(target.id);
}
//检查，若符合则移除错误样式
function check(target,regex){
    if(regex.test($.trim($(target).val()))){
       removeWrongColor($(target));
    }else{
	   addWrongColor($(target));
	}
}
//增加错误样式
function addWrongColor(target){
    target.attr("style"," background: none repeat scroll 0 0 #FDF8F8;border: 1px solid #E40000;");
}
//移除错误样式
function removeWrongColor(target){
    target.attr("style","display:inline");
}
//合并换行符
function mergeEnterKey(id){
	var str = $('#'+id).val();
	if(!!str){
		var parter=/(\n)+/g;
	    str = str.replace(parter,"\n");
	    $('#'+id).val(str);
	}
}

<script type="text/javascript" desc="新版图片上传接入">
SWFUP.picpath="/p2/big/,/p2/small/,/p2/tiny/";
SINGLEUP.picurl="p2";
$(document).ready(function(){
    UpImageShowBar.initBar({
       hazDetail:false,
       container:"uploadImgcontainer",
       imgMax:8,
       images:getPicValueForUpdate()
    }); 
});
//判断上传图片是否为空
function isPicEmpty(){
    var data = UpImageShowBar.getImgs();
    if(data == null || data.length == 0)
        return true;
    return false;
}
// 接收图片控件的值
function getPicValueForPost() {
    var pic = [];
    var tag = [];
    var desc = [];
    var data = UpImageShowBar.getImgs();
    if(data != null &amp;&amp; data.length &gt; 0) {
        $(data).each(function(i, n){
            // 标签
            var _tag = n.label;
            if(_tag == null) _tag = '';
            tag.push(_tag);

            // 图片路径
            var _url = n.url;
            _url = _url.replace('http://pic.58.com', '').replace('/tiny/', '/big/');
            pic.push(_url);
            desc.push(n.detail);
            // 描述
        });
    }
    return { "pic" : pic, "tag" : tag, "desc" : desc };
}

// 图片元素赋值
function setPicValueForPost() {
    var data = getPicValueForPost();
    $.bll.xiaobao.create('pic', data.pic.join('|'));
    $.bll.xiaobao.create('pictag', data.tag.join('|'));
    $(data.desc).each(function(i,n){
        var id = 'picdesc' + (++i);
        $.bll.xiaobao.create(id, n);
    });
}

// 获取图片数据用于修改时还原
function getPicValueForUpdate() {
    var data = [];
    if($('#pic').val().length &gt; 10) {
        var pic = $('#pic').val().split('|');
        var tag = $('#pictag').val().split('|');
        var desc = [];

        $(pic).each(function(i, n){
            var _tag = '';
            if(i &lt;= tag.length - 1) _tag = tag[i];
            data.push({'url': 'http://pic.58.com' + n, 'label':_tag, detail: $('#picdesc' + (i+1)).val()});
        });
    }

    return data;
    //{url:"http://pic.58.com/p1/tiny/n_19187650139921.jpg",label:"厨房",detail:"zzzz"}
}

$().ready(function(){
    $("#fabu").click(setPicValueForPost);
});
</script>
